Sadly most people have no clue about grading videos. There is no one colour, you adjust the levels to the values you want. Same goes for printing pictures. There is no true colour apart form pantone for print. but you are always going to have to choose colour range values from video. it may be darker or lighter, whichever suits the brief best. There is no true representation of colour. try taking a picture throughout the day from dusk till dawn. the colours will change even from global illumination and ambient occlusion. People just are very clueless about these everyday industry matters. why do you think lighting is so important in film? it sets the mood. Without it everything looks awful and you can't get the right shutters speeds etc....if you don't know you don't know, don't jump on hate bandwagons!
